    SELECT [r].[RestaurantName], [r].[RestaurantAddress], [m0].[MenuItemsItemID], [m0].[RestaurantsRestaurantID], [r].[RestaurantID]
    FROM [MenuItemsRestaurant] AS [m0]
    INNER JOIN [Restaurants] AS [r] ON [m0].[RestaurantsRestaurantID] = [r].[RestaurantID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ItemID] = [t0].[MenuItemsItemID]
ORDER BY [t].[Rating] DESC, [t].[ItemID], [t0].[MenuItemsItemID], [t0].[RestaurantsRestaurantID]
